def perform_tidl_unit_subprocess(tidl_offload : bool, run_infer : bool, test_name : str, test_suite : str, testdir_parent : str):
'''
Perform an tidl unit test using a subprocess (in order to properly capture output for fatal errors)
Called by perform_tidl_unit
'''

"test_suite" : test_suite,

p.start()

p.join(timeout=600)
if p.is_alive():
p.terminate()

def perform_tidl_unit_subprocess(tidl_offload : bool, run_infer : bool, test_name : str, test_suite : str, testdir_parent : str):
'''
Perform an tidl unit test using a subprocess (in order to properly capture output for fatal errors)
Called by perform_tidl_unit
'''

kwargs = {"tidl_offload" : tidl_offload,
"run_infer" : run_infer,
"test_name" : test_name,
"test_suite" : test_suite,
"testdir_parent" : testdir_parent}

p = Process(target=perform_tidl_unit_oneprocess, kwargs=kwargs)
p.start()


# Note: This timeout parameter must be lower than the pytest-timeout parameter
# passed to the pytest command (on the command line or in pytest.ini)
p.join(timeout=600)
if p.is_alive():
p.terminate()

# Cleanup leftover files
for f in glob.glob("/dev/shm/vashm_buff_*"):
os.remove(f)

def perform_tidl_unit_subprocess(tidl_offload : bool, run_infer : bool, test_name : str, test_suite : str, testdir_parent : str):
'''
Perform an tidl unit test using a subprocess (in order to properly capture output for fatal errors)
Called by perform_tidl_unit
'''

kwargs = {"tidl_offload" : tidl_offload,
"run_infer" : run_infer,
"test_name" : test_name,
"test_suite" : test_suite,
"testdir_parent" : testdir_parent}

p = Process(target=perform_tidl_unit_oneprocess, kwargs=kwargs)
p.start()


# Note: This timeout parameter must be lower than the pytest-timeout parameter
# passed to the pytest command (on the command line or in pytest.ini)
p.join(timeout=600)
if p.is_alive():
p.terminate()

# Cleanup leftover files
for f in glob.glob("/dev/shm/vashm_buff_*"):
os.remove(f)

def perform_tidl_unit_subprocess(tidl_offload : bool, run_infer : bool, test_name : str, test_suite : str, testdir_parent : str):
'''
Perform an tidl unit test using a subprocess (in order to properly capture output for fatal errors)
Called by perform_tidl_unit
'''

kwargs = {"tidl_offload" : tidl_offload,
"run_infer" : run_infer,
"test_name" : test_name,
"test_suite" : test_suite,
"testdir_parent" : testdir_parent}

p = Process(target=perform_tidl_unit_oneprocess, kwargs=kwargs)
p.start()


# Note: This timeout parameter must be lower than the pytest-timeout parameter
# passed to the pytest command (on the command line or in pytest.ini)
p.join(timeout=600)
if p.is_alive():
p.terminate()

# Cleanup leftover files
for f in glob.glob("/dev/shm/vashm_buff_*"):
os.remove(f)

def perform_tidl_unit_subprocess(tidl_offload : bool, run_infer : bool, test_name : str, test_suite : str, testdir_parent : str):
'''
Perform an tidl unit test using a subprocess (in order to properly capture output for fatal errors)
Called by perform_tidl_unit
'''

kwargs = {"tidl_offload" : tidl_offload,
"run_infer" : run_infer,
"test_name" : test_name,
"test_suite" : test_suite,
"testdir_parent" : testdir_parent}

p = Process(target=perform_tidl_unit_oneprocess, kwargs=kwargs)
p.start()


# Note: This timeout parameter must be lower than the pytest-timeout parameter
# passed to the pytest command (on the command line or in pytest.ini)
p.join(timeout=600)
if p.is_alive():
p.terminate()

# Cleanup leftover files
for f in glob.glob("/dev/shm/vashm_buff_*"):
os.remove(f)

def perform_tidl_unit_subprocess(tidl_offload : bool, run_infer : bool, test_name : str, test_suite : str, testdir_parent : str):
'''
Perform an tidl unit test using a subprocess (in order to properly capture output for fatal errors)
Called by perform_tidl_unit
'''

kwargs = {"tidl_offload" : tidl_offload,
"run_infer" : run_infer,
"test_name" : test_name,
"test_suite" : test_suite,
"testdir_parent" : testdir_parent}

p = Process(target=perform_tidl_unit_oneprocess, kwargs=kwargs)
p.start()


# Note: This timeout parameter must be lower than the pytest-timeout parameter
# passed to the pytest command (on the command line or in pytest.ini)
p.join(timeout=600)
if p.is_alive():
p.terminate()

# Cleanup leftover files
for f in glob.glob("/dev/shm/vashm_buff_*"):
os.remove(f)

def perform_tidl_unit_subprocess(tidl_offload : bool, run_infer : bool, test_name : str, test_suite : str, testdir_parent : str):
'''
Perform an tidl unit test using a subprocess (in order to properly capture output for fatal errors)
Called by perform_tidl_unit
'''

kwargs = {"tidl_offload" : tidl_offload,
"run_infer" : run_infer,
"test_name" : test_name,
"test_suite" : test_suite,
"testdir_parent" : testdir_parent}

p = Process(target=perform_tidl_unit_oneprocess, kwargs=kwargs)
p.start()


# Note: This timeout parameter must be lower than the pytest-timeout parameter
# passed to the pytest command (on the command line or in pytest.ini)
p.join(timeout=600)
if p.is_alive():
p.terminate()

# Cleanup leftover files
for f in glob.glob("/dev/shm/vashm_buff_*"):
os.remove(f)

def perform_tidl_unit_subprocess(tidl_offload : bool, run_infer : bool, test_name : str, test_suite : str, testdir_parent : str):
'''
Perform an tidl unit test using a subprocess (in order to properly capture output for fatal errors)
Called by perform_tidl_unit
'''

kwargs = {"tidl_offload" : tidl_offload,
"run_infer" : run_infer,
"test_name" : test_name,
"test_suite" : test_suite,
"testdir_parent" : testdir_parent}

p = Process(target=perform_tidl_unit_oneprocess, kwargs=kwargs)
p.start()


# Note: This timeout parameter must be lower than the pytest-timeout parameter
# passed to the pytest command (on the command line or in pytest.ini)
p.join(timeout=600)
if p.is_alive():
p.terminate()

# Cleanup leftover files
for f in glob.glob("/dev/shm/vashm_buff_*"):
os.remove(f)

def perform_tidl_unit_subprocess(tidl_offload : bool, run_infer : bool, test_name : str, test_suite : str, testdir_parent : str):
'''
Perform an tidl unit test using a subprocess (in order to properly capture output for fatal errors)
Called by perform_tidl_unit
'''

kwargs = {"tidl_offload" : tidl_offload,
"run_infer" : run_infer,
"test_name" : test_name,
"test_suite" : test_suite,
"testdir_parent" : testdir_parent}

p = Process(target=perform_tidl_unit_oneprocess, kwargs=kwargs)
p.start()


# Note: This timeout parameter must be lower than the pytest-timeout parameter
# passed to the pytest command (on the command line or in pytest.ini)
p.join(timeout=600)
if p.is_alive():
p.terminate()

# Cleanup leftover files
for f in glob.glob("/dev/shm/vashm_buff_*"):
os.remove(f)
